Acqua di Gio was created by Alberto Morillas, Annick Menardo and Christian Dussoulier. Top notes are Lime, Lemon, Bergamot, Jasmine, Orange, Mandarin Orange and Neroli; middle notes are Sea Notes, Jasmine, Calone, Rosemary, Peach, Freesia, Hiacynth, Cyclamen, Violet, Coriander, Rose, Nutmeg and Mignonette; base notes are White Musk, Cedar, Oakmoss, Patchouli and Amber. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Inspired by beauty of Pantellerie, where he spent his vacation, Armani created the aroma of Aqua di Gio for men and women. The fragrance for men is a scent of freedom, full of wind and water. The composition is built of a perfect harmony of sweet and salty notes of sea water and nuances of sunny warmth on your skin. Aqua di Gio is full of scorching Mediterranean sun. Bitter citrus with aromatic nuance of rosemary intertwines with salty, sea nuances and pellucid hedione. Sharp notes of spices are softened by woody base with warm, musky trail.</p>

<br />

And it has become so damn expensive too... Decided to purchase again out of nostalgia recently and its projection &amp; performance is pretty poor compared to what it used to be. As for the scent, idk if it’s the combination of the outdated profile and the cheap reformulation, but to me it’s almost unrecognizable. The citrus in the new batches is so synthetic I just get blasted with the synthetic citrus from the opening, that it’s all you can smell until it fades. I don’t know, maybe I got a bad bottle/batch, but I was disappointed in how it reminded nothing of the OG. <br />
<br />
Either way, there’s so many better “blue” fragrances on the market that give you more value for their price, that it makes it hard to recommend ADG outside of a nostalgic buy. I’d recommend Profundo over this for someone looking for something similar to the OG DNA, but with a more modern take and will last longer than 20 minutes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1370156">Afc_Croatian</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-01">08/01/24 06:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Acqua Di Gio in 2024.<br />
When I started my fragrance journey, I purchased this one early on. One way I like to measure how good a scent truly is for me is if it stands the test of time as I collect more scents. With ADG, the more I purchased, the more I loved this one.<br />
<br />
All it took was one spray for me to appreciate the citrus notes in this one: fresh lemon, neroli &amp; sea notes are what I pick up the most from this. I'm not going to lie &amp; say I can detect all 100 notes in this, but just know that the freshness is so pleasing on any day, especially a summer day or a relaxing one indoors.<br />
<br />
This has become my go-to scent when I am at home or running errands &amp; just want to smell clean without standing out, I know that every time I have passed someone with a nice citrus scent on I think wow that person smells so clean and I'm sure ADG will do that for you too.<br />
<br />
Despite owning over 100 scents, I went through a 100ml bottle and am currently 2/3 through my 300ml bottle, this fragrance is no joke &amp; easily blind-buy safe.<br />
A 300ml bottle is worth the investment since this lasts not even 3 hours on me and I respray throughout the day.<br />
<br />
A timeless scent, from a beautiful fragrance line.<br />
9.3/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2235588"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2235588#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2234537" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2024694">rsnero680</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-25">07/25/24 14:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Since my last review got downvoted to hell, let me rephrase my thoughts on this from a less attacking angle.<br />
I loved this smell from the tester card, hence why I got it. It was a great, fresh, citrusy-aquatic fragrance. However, I have 2 major issues that are enough to keep me from having it on my shelf:<br />
1) My own skin chemistry.<br />
When I sprayed it on my skin, it smelled very different than from the tester card. On me, this smells almost identical to Versace Pour Homme, which I already own, except with the lemon cranked up to 11. Because of this redundancy, I decided I wanted to get rid of it.<br />
2) The performance.<br />
Holy shit.<br />
I once sprayed this on myself 6 times, only for it to disappear within an hour. It also hardly projects at all on me if I sprayed a normal amount. I usually dismiss any complaints about reformulation (e.g. YSL La Nuit de L'Homme, D&amp;G The One, Dior Homme Intense), but this one is horrible. I don't want a "beast mode" fragrance, but it should last more than an hour.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2229335"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2229335#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2229108" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The opening left me questioning why it is so well loved in the fragrance community, but by the mid and dry down, I became a convert. This truly is a classic - mandarin citruses, floral notes of peach, roses, violets and hyacinths; a marine touch that makes me think of warmer weather; but the notes I feel that give this fragrance character are coriander, oakmoss and patchouli. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1415309">MrSpengler</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-03">07/03/24 19:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Disclaimer: I'm no expert, I'm just an aficionado with preferences; also, English is not my first languaje. <br />
<br />
I tried this in a sunny, dry, warm (27°C/~80°F), mild-windy day. <br />
<br />
Sharp alcohol and lime-bergamot opening; after a minute o two, the harshness disippates. Sea water, citrus, flowers; also some flowery/fruity sweetness. As minutes (~15) go on, it mellows down even more; it gets even more floral and, imo, losses it's marine character. After about an hour, only a intimate light flowery and skin-musky scent is left behind. <br />
<br />
Because it leans towards the flower side, I think it can be considered somewhat unisex, or at least, not traditionally masculine (which is not bad, it's just that); I believe some tobacco could give more masculinity and/or maturity (and it pairs good with flowers); smokers may have a 'better' experience. <br />
<br />
My biggest 'problem' with AdG is not the lightness or the flowers, but the lack of marine character; it is a chill, relaxed stroll in a flower field (with some sea at first), which is good, but it's not the coast trip I was told and hoped for.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I have a 2005 batch of this and it is good. Very classical,smooth,versatile,masculine.<br />
<br />
Even if you don't like citrus based fragrances, it is impossible to not like this one.<br />
<br />
Every uncle,dad,grandpa has this one but it still can be worn any summer day.<br />
<br />
Smell is to die for, truly a special fresh,citrusy fragrance.<br />
<br />
Smell- 10/10<br />
Longevity- 5/10(5 hours)<br />
Performance- 3/10( sadly)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2200101"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2200101#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2199842" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1791456">Toby Alexandru</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-22">05/22/24 11:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Can't lie, I love this. This has truly stood the test of time and still works just as well in 2024 as it did in the late 90's when it was released. Although it's best suited for spring and summer, it can easily be worn year round. It's not among MY personal favorite fragrances, but I find that older people (30+) absolutely LOVE this. Like whenever I wear this my mom always says "Oh, porți din nou acqua di gio" To my non Romanian people it translates to "Oh you're wearing Acqua Di Gio again!" She just loves it. My dad also used to wear Acqua Di Gio back in the day and i'd say that if you meet a guy over the age of 30, there's like a 50/50 that he's owned and worn Acqua Di Gio at least once in his lifetime.<br />
<br />
This scent of ADG itself appeals to all ages, but older people have that nostalgic factor playing in, which is why I'd say it probably leans a little older in terms of the age group this appeals to. If you're a young man and wanna "rizz" up a milf, this is prolly the fragrance you should be wearing.<br />
<br />
The performance is mid, but if you like me have a tendency to overspray, just make sure you spray at least 6 sprays on your neck, a couple sprays on your wrists and a few more sprays on your clothes and it should last you all day. The scent overall smells better on your skin than on clothes, but if you spray on both it'll give you better longevity and the difference is that noticeable. <br />
<br />
Overall: Certified hood classic / 10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2164323"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2164323#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2164180" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2065890">Jorjeyo Armstrongi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-12">04/12/24 22:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A bit of green at the start, but not nearly as much as the EDP or the Parfum. Some light citrus that is blended well enough to seem not super citrusy. Fresh, Aquatic, Soapy, Clean, a bit generic as well.. it can’t all be good. This is kind of is its own unique scent in that everything is so well blended together. There is a reason ADG has stood the test of time. This is a really good fragrance. <br />
<br />
I did buy this primarily for layering, but it is fine on its own. Unfortunately, the longevity is not very good - the projection dies down really fast. Also, be aware that there is a new 2024 formulation that has a gradient bottle. The description I left above was of the prior formulation with the completely opaque bottle. I bought this recently in 2024 from an online discounter, selling older stock, without realizing that there was a new formula that I could have bought instead.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/396740">valeri0706</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-06">04/06/24 04:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After 2 days of using my new EDT (2024 bottle with the new gradient and engraving re-positioning), I can safely say the OG EDT is back.<br />
<br />
Scent has been improved and it's now more sea-like and aromatic during the drydown, closer to the original release, compared to the heavier citrus undertone in the last few years' reformulation. The lemon cleaner scent from the OG's opening has been toned down, making the new release smell more natural.<br />
<br />
Longevity is also around 6-7 hours now, which is a major improvement over the previous release. Fantastic re-imagination of the most sold men fragrance of all time.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2116015"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2116015#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2114351" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2114351" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SiddhantSuryawanshi"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1690312"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1690312.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SiddhantSuryawanshi" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2114351ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2114351" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1690312">SiddhantSuryawanshi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-04">04/04/24 12:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It was in Japan, the winter of 2018, where the world glittered with a festive chill. Everything hummed with a different energy; the streets bright with holiday cheer &amp; the rush of shoppers. Back then, I saw her as a true friend; a brilliant, witty woman with a spark. <br />
<br />
At work, she was my boss, always pushing me to be better.  Sure, the intensity could be overwhelming at times, but I mistook it for genuine care.  That shopping trip was different, though, a glimpse of the playful side she hid beneath her usual professionalism. Even her gentle ribbing about my spending felt almost...sisterly.<br />
<br />
Then came the fragrance shop, not a planned destination, but a magnetic pull. Scents swirled with the potential of hidden stories. My fingers grazed the cool glass bottles, seeking something special. She watched, maybe sensing a desire in me to break out of my shell. <br />
<br />
Then it caught me; a scent that was both fresh and warm, like sunshine on a rippling ocean. Citrus played with spice, flowers adding a sweet mystery. It felt... vibrant. Alive. Like something I could become if I dared. <br />
<br />
"If you can spend this much on watches," she said, a smile in her voice, "a little on yourself never hurt anyone." The words felt like an unexpected stamp of approval, a touch of encouragement I desperately craved.<br />
<br />
Back then, I didn't know this was the start of my fascination with fragrances. I just knew that scent, the one I bought without hesitation, became a symbol of something new. It was the scent of possibility, of stepping into my own in a way I hadn't before. <br />
<br />
Of course, with time comes clarity. The playful banter turned to cutting remarks, her encouragement morphed into subtle manipulation. The woman I once admired revealed her true nature. Yet, that fragrance... it remains untainted. Women still compliment it, men still ask what it is.  <br />
<br />
And as the years unfold, I wear it with a mix of fondness and irony. It's a memento of that early time in Japan, of the naive belief that I'd found a genuine mentor. But it's also an evidence of the transformative power of scent; how it can outlast the very person who sparked your love for it. That fragrance, Acqua di Gio by Giorgio Armani, marks both the beginning of my exploration and the moment I realized that sometimes the greatest paths are walked alone.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; So happy to hear the 2024 bottle of the EDT has been reformulated for the better as the OG is one of my most favourite fragrances ever. I will probably get the new release soon.<br />
<br />
Whatever Armani has done with the new 2024 bottles, it seems to have been an overall improvement as the new 2024 gradient bottle I got of ADG Parfum has also been tweaked to resemble Profumo closer than the 2023 bottle did. They even added the signature magnetic cap and have amped up the incense note, making the opening fresher and the drydown even more amazing.<br />
<br />
I can see they've put the old bottle releases on sale on the Armani UK website, so I can only presume they are slowly phasing them out, leaving only the 2024 releases. It was everywhere. Girls adored it and was one of my signature frags from 2001-2006. I still have my old Cosmair bottle and wear it from time to time. I don’t know what today’s formulation smells like and don’t want to know. I will never buy another bottle of this because my bottle will last till I pass away. I do wear it from time to time and am immediately blissed-out. It’s stunning from morning till night. The Cosmair EDT is nuclear and sooo dense….as were most EDT’s from this era. <br />
<br />
The memories that come back to me when I wear this were some of the best and worst memories of my life….but I can wear this today with a big smile on my face because the past is in the past. <br />
<br />
Cheers!!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2102874"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2102874#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2102611" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1923250">LePianoMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-24">03/24/24 08:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Mainly bright citrus on the opening mixed with sea water/marine notes with noticeable saltiness, and a white musk underlying it all and adding some maturity.<br />
<br />
I don’t understand why people say this is “old”, though. The citrus and sea water give it a bright, refreshing feel and really it’s the musk that brings you down back to earth and what gives this the amazing versatility it has. <br />
<br />
Btw, this may not be a beast when it comes to longevity but it’s an EDT- it’s not supposed to be. Do NOT overspray this. I normally do 4 sprays of basically any perfume, 2 if they’re super strong, and it had been a while since I’d worn ADG EDT. Applied 6 sprays and gosh it’s strong. My mom could smell me from 3 feet away, and it wasn’t like she could barely smell me, she described it as being “bombarded” by my scent. This shit is strong hahaha, be smart about how much you apply and keep a decant with you to apply again around mid day or early afternoon.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Fragrance Rating - 9 / 10<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1544521">0xrafae</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-18">03/18/24 07:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The opening notes section could serve as a Wikipedia page for every citrus note imaginable. Looking at the number of middle notes, I'm genuinely surprised that Aqua di Gio manages to maintain any coherence. This may be because to the authors kept themselves more restrained at the base notes level—but only in the context of the other layers. Somehow, out of this chaos, one of the most iconic perfumes ever was born. I bet that the odds of this happening were as high as of a plane assembling itself after a massive explosion in a garbage dump.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The longevity and projection is not not the best though, only lasting you a couple of hours, and requiring several sprays.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2083277"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2083277#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2081808" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2081762" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="rizzard"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1930662"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1930662.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="rizzard" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2081762ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2081762" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1930662">rizzard</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-04">03/04/24 08:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Read @Jecmenn review. It's spot on. I order a 1.7oz and a 6.7oz from ebay. Different shippers. While both smell fresh, the 6.7oz goes straight from a fresh and clean to a woody scent, then is gone in an hour. The 1.7floz I ordered starts fresh and clean except with a distinct floral hue. It smells like a designer cologne at the start, then dries down to the floral notes while maintaining the masculine tones. It last longer, has higher sillage, and greater staying power on the skin.<br />
<br />
I thought it might just be the skin scent mixing with the colognes, but after testing on paper strips, I can definitely say the juice in the 6.7oz and 1.7oz are different. I go nose-blind after the first sniff with the 6.7oz, and not till 5-6 sniffs with the 1.7. Not to mention the 6.7oz is slightly more yellow than the almost white 1.7oz. <br />
<br />
Just a word of caution. Although I will say the scent of both are pleasant, the only colognes I have that I've been compliment on (out of the ~15 others I own), and is an extremely safe blind buy for a newbie.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It smells very citrusy and smells really good for the money. A good way to say it is to call the Profumo the big brother were it’s not quite as sweet but it still smells a lot like each other. I would recommend this still over the Profumo but that’s just my opinion. If it matters a lot to you that it lasts long then I would definitely recommend buying the Profumo. To me it matters a lot that it lasts long but with this great smell then I don’t really care as much as normally. If you don’t like the Profumo and still want something similar to ADG then I would suggest buying the le beau which is my favourite summer fragrance. The le beau is just as sweet as the ADG. I think that both lives up to the ideal summer fragrance. If it’s about the money then you should buy ADG but if it’s about the quality then it’s the le beau. Thanks to anyone that had the courage to read all this and I tried my best to help.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2077736"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2077736#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2077641" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1159639">Jecmenn</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-26">02/26/24 10:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've been wearing this perfume for years now (mainly because it is the only perfume that does not trigger my wife's migraines) and I can say that something about the formulation had to change very recently. <br />
<br />
In the past the scent was very straightforward, starting with a nice blend of mild citrus and marine tones, which slowly turned into more floral notes, and the dry down stabilized with musky tones with a slight hint of citruses and marine notes.<br />
However, the last bottle I bought (200ml), seems to have something different about it. The top is very similar to the old batches with a heavy emphasis on citruses and sea notes, however as it dries down, there are no floral notes, it goes straight into this woody, almost smoky note that wasn't present at all in the previous batches I had. The woodiness lingers on the skin for a very long time. Unfortunately, the scent turns sour with time and I swear I can even smell something like pickled vegetables at times after 6+ hours on the skin.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2073829" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Mage4Zelda"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1997529"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1997529.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="Mage4Zelda" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2073829ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2073829" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1997529">Mage4Zelda</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-25">02/25/24 13:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The classic, vintage and popular from the 90s. I wish I could part ways but this fragrance is just put together too well.<br />
<br />
From the opening to the base notes, this is a fragrance that does it all in a consistent, mellow and subtle style that declares warmth and freshness of spring and summer, without being too floral, soapy and aromatic. Gio EDT is a citrus scent that opens with good projection and composition of lemon-orange-jasmine giving way to sweet aquatic citrus and floral notes, without the bitterness associated with citrus fruits. This combination steadily and ultimately settles down to floral-musk so ingeniously and admirably that it evokes a feeling of genuine leather on skin. Even through the dry down, the scent gives off pleasant and considerable citrus vibes, making it distinguished and easily recognizable by its name after hours of initial spray. A subtle and appreciable note of jasmine, with a hint of sweet lemon, becomes perceptible as the scent fades away. <br />
<br />
Ideal for summer days, warmer temperatures seem to mystically enhance the projection and sillage of this fragrance. The subtlety of this fragrance, sillage, composition and presentation of its notes makes AdG EDT a reliable and outstanding performer. This is what GIO delivers successfully, making it a fragrance that still retains its value after almost 30 years of its conception. <br />
<br />
Acqua Di Gio, EDT is one of my favourite fresh-citrus scents and my first buy. Must I mention that the chemistry from the bottle that I own from 2005 is still as potent as the first spray. A very safe and reliable bet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2073829"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2073829#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2072630" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Then about 5 years ago i decided to go on a journey to discover what i would like better. I noticed over the years since maybe 2017ish that the profile of ADG seems more diluted or lighter. I know some people hate or deny hearing that older batches are better, but I have a 2010 and 2013 bottle and they both pop better than a newer travel size bottle I bought last year. It's not even close. The older bottles have this stronger zest, orange, and some other note I can't figure out. It's not a projection banger, but if it's an older bottle of ADG it's still in my top 10, and I've tried hundreds to date. Anyone with a teenage boy I'd recommend getting this for them as a starter.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2070247"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2070247#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2069552" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I wish that it was a bit juicier or more authentic.<br />
Very clean with some cheap body wash / dish detergent vibes.<br />
<br />
The middle is also just as boring. The floral notes in here are completely lost in the dihydromyrcenol. Missing a distinct, star of the show note. <br />
<br />
The base is amber/woody but feels like an afterthought.<br />
<br />
I will say the dry down is nicer than the opening where some of the initial vague sharpness builds a bit more character.<br />
<br />
Verdict:<br />
It’s not offensive. Just feels dull and corporate. Just smells like walking into the men’s fragrance section at a department store.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2068197"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2068197#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2067451" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; To me personally? I really wouldn't buy this fragrance. It's kind of boring, doesn't last long, and doesn't make you stand out. <br />
<br />
However, man on man. I have gotten TIMELESS compliments from how good I smell with this thing. It almost makes me laugh at how sometimes I won't get anything with some of the better fragrances and more expensive ones I own, yet this one that is the OG Acqua De Gio will almost land me a compliment every single time I wear it. <br />
<br />
If I were you, I'd buy this if you were a beginner or somebody who appreciates classic fragrances. It doesn't make sense how this is my most complimented, but man on man does it do the job. <br />
<br />
Overall rating: 10/10. <br />
<br />
I personally think there's better choices out there. But this does the job of impressing others better than every cologne I own.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="2067451"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=2067451#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2066382" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I was so enamoured with the scent immediately pulled him to the side to ask what he was wearing. The next day I headed to the mall cuz I had to have this scent. No perfume before or since has had the same impression I got from this. Fast forward 20+ years I'm finally getting around to checking out the modern formula. It was very disappointing because it just doesn't seem to have the it factor it once had. Don't get me wrong it smells great and is quite potent the first few hours, but it lost some of its sharpness which is what I adored from this fragrance, now without that sharpness it comes across as slightly too sweet for my taste. After it dries down I get what I'd call a shadow of the true og scent in the background of the fragrance. Getting past nostalgia and my disappointment, this actually performed much better than expected after hearing the reviews, and smells amazing despite losing some of its magic, which really goes to show you that this is a true masterpiece in that despite its former glorious formula, still smells better than 90 percent of modern designer fragrance . 9.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The mere thought of hooking up with a guy wearing this would probably be a deal-breaker for me, as shallow as that sounds.<br />
<br />
Aquatics and citrus based scents don't go down too well with me. I find Acqua di Gio sharp and irritating. There are some citrus masculines I adore, for example, Acqua di Parma's Colonia and L'eau d'Issey pour Homme, yet this incredibly popular fragrance just can't, and will not appeal to my tastes.<br />
<br />
The opening is heavy with citrus accords, most notably lemon, lime and bergamot. To my nose these notes are not crisp nor refreshing, but rather astringent and metallic. The ocean water note makes matters worse, introducing an odd and somewhat clashing salt accord.<br />
<br />
Acqua di Gio is the masculine equivalent to D&amp;G Light Blue for Women. Both fragrances are popular citrus scents that fall into either a love it or hate it category. <br />
<br />
Perhaps in a gym or a sports situation, Acqua di Gio is tolerable, however I find too many guys wearing this during Winter, out clubbing, or in the worst case scenario, applying it far too heavily which leaves me gasping for air. It's a Summer fragrance and should be worn casually, in moderate doses.<br />
<br />
Due to its popularity and expensive price tag, I know many men will buy it thinking it's the best smelling thing in the world and that it attracts women like bees to a honey pot. Marketing is not always accurate. Sniff around before putting your cash on the register for this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="226808"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=226808#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent355557" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/410918">wesleyhclark</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2013-04-12">04/12/13 05:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Clean/fresh/oceanic/citrus... it's not my thing. In the words of Luca Turin, it's one of those fragrances for men who don't like fragrances and who suspect none of their friends do, either. <br />
<br />
How overly popular is this fragrance? <br />
<br />
1.) You can buy a little packet of this in the D.C. Zoo men's room for 75 cents. (So you don't smell like a resident of the Great Ape House.) <br />
<br />
2.) The number of reviews on this particular page cause my PC to run slow.<br />
<br />
--------<br />
<br />
Okay, I needed some summer scents to make my wardrobe more diverse, so I traded a 1 oz. bottle of Tsar for a 1 oz. bottle of this. Number me among the billions who wear it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="410"comment_id="355557"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-410.html?ccid=355557#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent505569" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
